Good looks at one bright male McCown's (chestnut shoulder patch, black bib on an otherwise clear gray breast), and 1-2 duller birds that I think were winter-plumaged males.  Whenever the flocks flushed, I could usually pick out atleast one longspur by either hearing a rattle call (Lapland) or by observing the unique white tail pattern (McCown's).  When the flock was close to the road, I observed one female Chestnut-collared Longspur, and I also heard some rattle calls that were not Lapland but that I believe were this species.
